#campusüèõ

Toska - noun /Ààt≈ç-sk…ô/ - Russian word roughly translated as sadness, melancholia, lugubriousness.

"No single word in English renders all the shades of toska. At its deepest and most painful, it is a sensation of great spiritual anguish, often without any specific cause. At less morbid levels it is a dull ache of the soul, a longing with nothing to long for, a sick pining, a vague restlessness, mental throes, yearning. In particular cases it may be the desire for somebody of something specific, nostalgia, love-sickness. At the lowest level it grades into ennui, boredom.

I've come to realize that nothing in life has inherent meaning (sounds nihilistic, I know). Money, for example, only holds value because we assign it so, using it to survive by exchanging it for essentials like food and water. Yet, somehow, it has also become an instrument of greed and suffering.

Everyone experiences suffering, though in different forms and intensities. No one is exempt from it. What can we do about this? We have two choices: either avoid the pain or accept it. Avoiding it is like living with a thorn lodged in you‚Äîover time, it festers and continues to hurt. Accepting it, on the other hand, is like removing the thorn and walking a path filled with more thorns, knowing that pain is simply part of life.

If you believe in reincarnation, this cycle of suffering will repeat itself, bound by fate and karma. True freedom comes when we stop letting suffering blind us. To do so, we must let go of our obsessions and learn to embrace the pain that comes with life.

#adviceüó£Ô∏è

Dear song lyric spammers,

We get it. There are some songs out there that really hype you and make you feel you can do anything. Songs that speak to your soul. Songs that make you just want to share the lyrics with everyone you know.

Still, it is hard for most people to share the same feelings as you when it comes out of context in the form of a confession post, and I speak for most of us in saying that the recent flood of song lyrics has gotten out of hand. For you, the lyrics carry deep and powerful meanings, for the rest of us, it is a large wall of text that is obstructive and annoying to scroll through. You could literally just say "check out XXX song it is üî•üî•" and it would be so much better than copying the entire chunk of lyrics here.

So either:
1) you really love the song

2) you are a troll that delights in making the lives of the smu community miserable as we have to take extra effort to scroll through a post that you know we will never bother to read

3) you are in a really bad situation right now and the songs you share are your only avenue of comfort. In which case, I'm sorry to hear that you are going through this, but there are better ways and outlets of expressing your feelings.

In any case, please stop spamming lyrics in this page. Thank you ‚ù§Ô∏è‚ù§Ô∏è
